## Mod Showcase: Fallout NV Modlist

List of mods used in my Fallout New Vegas streams
[Twitch](https://www.twitch.tv/fleenfleen)
[YouTube](https://www.youtube.com/@FleenStreams)

## Fallout:	New Vegas Mods

<hr />
*THIS LIST IS FOR REFERENCE ONLY! DO NOT DOWNLOAD ALL OF THESE AND EXPECT IT TO WORK*

### (Sound)_Animal_Sounds 2

This mod adds various animal sounds to the exterior wasteland. It also fixes Ambient Wasteland 2.

### 00 - Improved Male Vanilla Body - FOMOD Installer 2.3

> By zzjay and 7thNighthawk for Fallout:	New Vegas (Default)

High poly, improved and SEAMLESS version of the male body.<br />Compatible with VANILLA outfits, and has actual feet instead of blocks, thanks to Robert's.<br />High resolution body and face textures that ensure seamless bodies for all races.<br />Released for the 10th anniversary of Fallout New Vegas.

### 1. Butcher Pete Complete - A Melee Animation Overhaul (Hitman Locomotion) 1.0

Installed 19/10/2023 from [Nexus Mods](https://www.nexusmods.com/newvegas/mods/79146/) (Animation) 

<img src="https://staticdelivery.nexusmods.com/mods/130/images/79146/79146-1669915949-1054236094.jpeg" alt="mod-image" height="350" />

> By rockbiter68 for Fallout:	New Vegas (Default)

A comprehensive melee animation overhaul for almost every single one-handed melee weapon in New Vegas, its DLCs, and TTW.<br /><br />Chop, slice, and bludgeon that Pete.




<hr />

### Consistent Pip-boy Icons v4 4.5

Installed 24/11/2025 from [Nexus Mods](https://www.nexusmods.com/newvegas/mods/65046/) (Bug Fixes) 

<img src="https://staticdelivery.nexusmods.com/mods/130/images/65046/65046-1652354812-1299390990.png" alt="mod-image" height="350" />

> By ItsMeJesusHChrist also known as LOC or The Icon Guy for Fallout:	New Vegas (Default)

This is a lore-friendly, mostly hand-drawn, total overhaul mod that tweaks around 3600 icons. They are immersively more consistent in terms of coloring and transparency. There are other bug fixes too, and many new details! Okay, just write that in the brief overview, it's not that hard.




<hr />

### 1. Wasteland Warrior - A Melee Animation Overhaul (Hitman Locomotion) 1.0

Installed 23/10/2023 from [Nexus Mods](https://www.nexusmods.com/newvegas/mods/80277/) (Animation) 

<img src="https://staticdelivery.nexusmods.com/mods/130/images/80277/80277-1678035012-1191569565.jpeg" alt="mod-image" height="350" />

> By rockbiter68 for Fallout:	New Vegas (Default)

Reanimates all animations for all two-handed melee weapon in the game. Yes, all of them. Zero balance changes: vanilla timings and power attack rules are applied.<br /><br />Requires kNVSE.

### UIO - User Interface Organizer 2.30

> By jazzisparis for Fallout:	New Vegas (Default)

An NVSE-powered plugin that is designed to manage and maintain all UI/HUD extensions added to the game by various mods. Once installed, UIO will ensure UI extensions are always properly installed and, when necessary, properly removed; it will automatically detect, resolve and prevent UI-related issues, and will help keep the game's UI intact.
